## 2026-06-16

### 业务流程图中“退货/退料”单据图标调整，统一实物对象风格

**修改文件：**
- client/src/config/flowConfig.ts

**具体说明：**
- 将销售退货（SR）的图标从 RefreshLeft 改为了 Box（代表货物退回到仓库）。
- 将采购退货（PR）的图标从 RefreshRight 改为了 Van（代表退货发送给供应商）。
- 将退料单（PJ）的图标从 RefreshLeft 改为了 Box（代表生产材料退回到仓库）。

**原因：**
- 原先的退货和退料单据使用的图标是代表“刷新/撤销”的抽象箭头图标（RefreshLeft / RefreshRight），而业务流程图上的其他单据（如货车、票据、箱子等）都是具象的实物。抽象图标显得格格不入，因此统一替换为具象的实物图标以贴合整站风格并更好地传达物理流向。

**影响范围：**
- 纯前端 UI 调整，无需重启后端。

### 修复分组导航页（流程图）相同路由不同查询参数导致节点显示为同一项的缺陷

**修改文件：**
- client/src/views/components/ProcessFlow.vue

**具体说明：**
- **现象**：在“销售管理”等采用流程图布局的导航页中，所有的节点标题全部显示为“报价单”（或第一个单据类型）。
- **修复**：更新了 ProcessFlow.vue 中的 indMenuItem 方法。原本的方法中使用了逻辑或 (||) 直接导致 find 函数在遇到基础路由相同时直接返回 true，忽略了 query 参数（如 ?doc_type=SQ 等）。将其修改为优先尝试完全匹配（包含路径和 query 参数），在没有完全匹配时，才降级使用基础路径匹配。

**原因：**
- JavaScript 的 ind 结合短路求值导致了所有具有相同 base path（如 /scm/docs）的节点匹配到了配置列表里的第一个项目。

**影响范围：**
- 纯前端 UI 修复，解决了销售、采购、生产、委外等分组下流程图标题显示重复的问题。无需重启后端。

### 淇椤堕儴闈㈠寘灞戝鑸樉绀洪敊璇殑鍗曟嵁绫诲瀷

  2. 鏃ヨ璐﹁鑷甫鐜伴噾绉戠洰 `account_code`锛屽嚟璇侀噷 `account_code` 鈮?璇ョ幇閲戠鐩€佷笖**鎭板ソ涓€鏉?*鐨勫垎褰曞嵆鏂板鏂圭鐩紱
  3. `UPDATE cashier_journal SET counter_account=?, voucher_year/month/type/no=鏂板€糮鈥斺€?*浠呭洖鍐欏鏂圭鐩?*锛屼笉鍔ㄩ噾棰?鎽樿锛涘彿鎴栨棩鏈熻嫢鏀逛簡鍒欏悓姝ュ埛鏂伴摼鎺ュ瓧娈碉紝閬垮厤涓嬫澶遍厤锛?  4. 鎵句笉鍒板叧鑱旇銆佹垨瀵规柟鍒嗗綍涓嶅敮涓€鏃堕潤榛樿烦杩囷紙杩斿洖 `updated:0`锛夛紝涓嶅奖鍝嶅嚟璇佷繚瀛樸€?- 鎺ュ叆鐐癸細`PUT /voucher/vouchers/:id` 鏇存柊浜嬪姟瀹屾垚鍚庯紝`if (voucher.source === 'cashier')` 璋冪敤鍥炲啓锛屽鐢ㄥ凡鏌ュ嚭鐨?`entryRows`锛沗try/catch` 瀹归敊锛堜笌鏃㈡湁 `syncCashierFromVoucher` 鍚岄鏍硷級銆?*涓嶅彈** `cashier:auto_sync` 寮€鍏抽檺鍒躲€?- 鍓嶇锛氳崏绋垮垪琛ㄣ€岀姸鎬併€嶅垪涓?`source==='cashier'` 鐨勫嚟璇佽拷鍔犱竴涓?plain 榛勮壊銆屽嚭绾炽€嶅皬鏍囩锛屼究浜庡湪鑽夌鍫嗛噷蹇€熻瘑鍒嚭绾虫寕璐﹀嚟璇併€?- **鐜伴噾/閾惰鍒嗗綍閿佸畾锛堥檺瀹氬彧鑳芥敼瀵规柟绉戠洰锛?*锛?  - 鍚庣 PUT 瀹堝崼锛歚voucher.source==='cashier'` 鏃讹紝姣斿缂栬緫鍓嶅悗銆岀幇閲?閾惰鍒嗗綍绛惧悕銆?`account_id|direction|amount`)锛屽嚒鐜伴噾/閾惰绉戠洰鍒嗗綍鐨勭鐩€佹柟鍚戞垨閲戦琚敼鍔ㄥ嵆杩斿洖 400銆屽嚭绾崇敓鎴愮殑鍑瘉鍙兘淇敼瀵规柟锛堟寕璐︼級绉戠洰锛岀幇閲?閾惰绉戠洰鍒嗗綍涓嶈兘鏀瑰姩銆嶃€?  - 鍓嶇 `VoucherEntryForm`锛氱紪杈戝嚭绾冲嚟璇侊紙`mode==='edit' && form.source==='cashier'`锛夋椂锛岀幇閲?閾惰鍒嗗綍锛坄is_cash=1||is_bank=1`锛夌殑绉戠洰鏀逛负鍙骞舵樉绀恒€岀幇閲戠鐩烽攣瀹氥€嶆爣绛撅紝鍊熻捶閲戦杈撳叆绂佺敤锛屽垹闄ゆ寜閽鐢紱鍏朵綑锛堝鏂?鎸傝处锛夊垎褰曞彲姝ｅ父缂栬緫銆?  - `VoucherForm` 鏂板 `source` 瀛楁锛岀敱 `loadVoucher` 浠庡嚟璇佸啓鍏ワ紝渚涜〃鍗曞垽鏂潵婧愩€傚鍒跺嚟璇侊紙mode='add'锛変笉鍙楅攣瀹氬奖鍝嶃€?

   - 鍑瘉绠＄悊琛ㄦ牸鎸?鍑瘉 + 鍒嗗綍"灞曞钩锛屾瀯寤鸿鐢?`{ ...v, ...e, _voucherId: v.id }`锛?*鍒嗗綍鐨?`id` 鐩存帴瑕嗙洊鍑瘉 `id`**锛涘彧鏈?`_voucherId` 鏄湡姝ｇ殑鍑瘉 ID銆?   - 鍏跺畠鍗曟潯/鎵归噺鎿嶄綔锛坄audit`/`unAudit`/`post`/`unPost`/`batchUnAudit`/`batchPost`/`batchUnpost`锛変竴寰嬬敤 `row._voucherId || row.id`锛涘敮鐙?`batchAudit` 鍐欐垚 `r.id || r._voucherId`锛屾案杩滄嬁鍒板垎褰?id锛屽鑷存彁浜ゅ埌鍚庣鐨勫叏鏄?entry id銆?   - 淇锛氭敼涓?`r._voucherId || r.id`锛涘苟鎸?voucher 鍘婚噸锛岄伩鍏嶅鍒嗗綍灞曞钩鏃舵妸鍚屼竴寮犲嚟璇侀噸澶嶅彂閫併€?

   - `/voucher/vouchers/batch-audit` 鐢?`results.push({ success: false, error })` 鍚炴帀鍗曟潯澶辫触锛屾渶鍚庢棤璁烘垚鍔熸暟鏄惁涓?0 閮借繑鍥?`code: 0` + `鎵归噺瀹℃牳瀹屾垚锛氭垚鍔?0 寮狅紝澶辫触 N 寮燻銆?   - 鍓嶇 `request.ts` 鎷︽埅鍣ㄥ彧鐪?HTTP 鐘舵€佺爜锛屼笉鐪嬩笟鍔?`code`锛屼簬鏄洿鎺ヨ蛋 success 鍒嗘敮锛屽脊鍑?鎵归噺瀹℃牳鎴愬姛"銆?   - 淇锛氬綋 `successCount === 0 && failCount > 0` 鏃惰繑鍥?HTTP 400 + 棣栦釜閿欒銆?

**鍏蜂綋璇存槑锛?*
- `getRequestIp` 鍦ㄥ彧鎷垮埌 `127.0.0.1`銆乣::1` 绛夊洖鐜湴鍧€鏃讹紝鑷姩璇诲彇鏈嶅姟鍣ㄧ墿鐞嗙綉鍗＄殑灞€鍩熺綉 IPv4 浣滀负鏄剧ず鍜屽瓨鍌?IP銆?- 灞€鍩熺綉 IP 閫夋嫨鏃朵紭鍏堟帓闄?VMware銆乂irtualBox銆乄SL銆丏ocker銆丠yper-V 绛夎櫄鎷熺綉鍗★紝浼樺厛浣跨敤鐪熷疄浠ュお缃?Wi-Fi 鍦板潃銆?- 鐧诲綍鎺ュ彛杩斿洖 `lastLoginIp`銆乣activeLoginIp`銆乣forcedOldLoginIp` 鍓嶇粺涓€閫氳繃 `toDisplayIp` 杞崲锛屽巻鍙插凡淇濆瓨鐨?`127.0.0.1` 涔熶細鍦ㄢ€滀笂涓€娆＄櫥褰曗€濆拰鈥滄槸鍚﹀己鍒剁櫥褰曗€濇彁绀轰腑鏄剧ず涓哄眬鍩熺綉 IP銆?- 鏂板 `requestIp` 鍗曞厓娴嬭瘯锛岃鐩?IPv6 鏄犲皠鍦板潃銆佸洖鐜湴鍧€璇嗗埆銆佸洖鐜湴鍧€鏄剧ず杞崲鍜岀湡瀹炲眬鍩熺綉 IP 鍘熸牱杩斿洖銆?
**鍘熷洜锛?*

- 鎵嬪姩鎵ц锛歚ALTER TABLE accounts ADD COLUMN require_cash_flow INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;`

**娴嬭瘯缁撴灉锛?*
浣跨敤 `/Users/luojun/projects/cw/妯＄増/鏂颁紒涓氫細璁″噯鍒?鏂颁紒涓氫細璁″噯鍒?acd` 娴嬭瘯瀵煎叆鎴愬姛锛?- 鉁?绉戠洰绾у埆璇嗗埆姝ｇ‘锛歚2221`(1绾? 鈫?`2221001`(2绾? 鈫?`2221001001`(3绾?
- 鉁?鐖跺瓙鍏崇郴姝ｇ‘锛歚2221001001` 鐨勭埗绾ф槸 `2221001`锛宍2221001` 鐨勭埗绾ф槸 `2221`
- 鉁?閰嶇疆鍖栬绠楋細鑷姩璇诲彇 account_code_lengths 閰嶇疆 `[4,3,3,2,2,2]`
- 鉁?瀵煎叆缁熻锛?45涓鐩紝245鏉℃湡鍒濅綑棰濓紝38涓姤琛ㄦā鏉?
**楠岃瘉鏂规硶锛?*
```sql
-- 楠岃瘉绉戠洰绾у埆
SELECT code, name, level FROM accounts WHERE code IN ('2221', '2221001', '2221001001');

-- 楠岃瘉鐖跺瓙鍏崇郴
SELECT a.code, a.name, a.level, p.code as parent_code
FROM accounts a
LEFT JOIN accounts p ON a.parent_id = p.id
WHERE a.level > 1
ORDER BY a.code;

-- 楠岃瘉杈呭姪鏍哥畻
SELECT code, name, is_aux, aux_types, require_cash_flow
FROM accounts
WHERE is_aux = 1 OR require_cash_flow = 1;
```

### 2. 鏁村悎鐧诲綍鐣岄潰鐨勯噸澶嶅鍏ユ寜閽?
**淇敼鏂囦欢锛?*
- `client/src/views/Login.vue` - 鐧诲綍椤甸潰缁勪欢
- `server/src/routes/auth.ts` - 鍚庣璺敱锛堟枃浠跺ぇ灏忛檺鍒讹級
- `server/src/scripts/importAcdToCurrentAccountSet.ts` - ACD鐢ㄦ埛瀵煎叆閫昏緫

     ```typescript
     // 鎵归噺鏌ヨ鍑芥暟
     export function getBatchBalances(
       db: BalanceQueryDb,
       accountSetId: string,
       accountCodes: string[],
       year: number,
       period: number
     ): Map<string, number> {
       const placeholders = accountCodes.map(() => '?').join(',')

       // 涓€娆℃€ф煡璇㈡墍鏈夌鐩殑鏈熷垵浣欓
       const initBalances = db.prepare(`
         SELECT a.code, SUM(ib.init_balance) as init_balance, a.direction
         FROM init_balances ib
         JOIN accounts a ON a.id = ib.account_id
         WHERE ib.account_set_id=? AND a.code IN (${placeholders}) AND ib.year=?
         GROUP BY a.code, a.direction
       `).all(accountSetId, ...accountCodes, year)

       // 涓€娆℃€ф煡璇㈡墍鏈夌鐩殑鏈熼棿浣欓
       const periodBalances = db.prepare(`
         SELECT a.code, SUM(ab.current_debit) as current_debit,
                SUM(ab.current_credit) as current_credit, a.direction
         FROM account_balances ab
         JOIN accounts a ON a.id = ab.account_id
         WHERE ab.account_set_id=? AND a.code IN (${placeholders})
           AND ab.year=? AND ab.period<=?
         GROUP BY a.code, a.direction
       `).all(accountSetId, ...accountCodes, year, period)

       // 璁＄畻鏈€缁堜綑棰濆苟缂撳瓨
       // ...
       return balanceMap
     }
     ```

     ```typescript
     let abortController: AbortController | null = null

     onBeforeUnmount(() => {
       if (searchTimer) clearTimeout(searchTimer)
       if (abortController) abortController.abort()
     })

     async function fetchData() {
       if (abortController) {
         abortController.abort()
       }
       abortController = new AbortController()
       const signal = abortController.signal

       try {
         const [accRes, catRes, auxRes] = await Promise.all([
           request.get<any[]>('/base/accounts', { params, signal }),
           request.get<any[]>('/base/aux-categories', { signal }),
           request.get<any[]>('/base/aux-items', { signal }),
         ])
         // ... 鏇存柊鐘舵€?       } catch (err: any) {
         if (err.name === 'AbortError' || err.name === 'CanceledError') {
           return
         }
         throw err
       }
     }
     ```

   function onSelect(selection: any[]) {
     selected.value = selection
     const selectableRows = flatList.value.filter(isSelectableRow)
     const isCurrentPageFullSelected = selection.length > 0 && selection.length === selectableRows.length

     // 鍏ㄩ€夊綋鍓嶉〉鏃讹紝鏄剧ず纭瀵硅瘽妗?     if (isCurrentPageFullSelected && pagination.total > pagination.pageSize && !selectAllMode.value) {

   }

### 2. 杈呭姪鏄庣粏璐︽煡璇㈡€ц兘浼樺寲锛圢+1 鏌ヨ闂锛?

    itemsByCategory.set(item.category_code, [])
  }
  itemsByCategory.get(item.category_code)!.push(item)

2. **鎵归噺 COUNT 鏌ヨ**
```typescript
for (const [categoryCode, categoryItems] of itemsByCategory) {
  // SQLite 鍙傛暟闄愬埗涓?999锛岄渶瑕佸垎鎵?  const batchSize = 900
  for (let i = 0; i < categoryItems.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = categoryItems.slice(i, i + batchSize)
    const itemIds = batch.map(item => item.id)

    // 浣跨敤 IN 瀛愬彞涓€娆℃€ф煡璇㈠涓緟鍔╅」鐩?    const countSql = `
      SELECT COUNT(*) as count
      FROM voucher_entries ve
      JOIN vouchers v ON v.id = ve.voucher_id
      WHERE json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.id') IN (${itemIds.map(() => '?').join(',')})
        AND ... (鍏朵粬绛涢€夋潯浠?
    `
    totalCount += db.prepare(countSql).get(...itemIds).count
  }
}
```

3. **鎵归噺鍒濆浣欓鏌ヨ**
```typescript
for (const [categoryCode, categoryItems] of itemsByCategory) {
  const batchSize = 900
  for (let i = 0; i < categoryItems.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = categoryItems.slice(i, i + batchSize)
    const itemIds = batch.map(item => item.id)

    const initSql = `
      SELECT COALESCE(SUM(CASE
        WHEN ve.direction = 'debit' THEN ve.amount
        ELSE -ve.amount
      END), 0) as init_balance
      FROM voucher_entries ve
      JOIN vouchers v ON v.id = ve.voucher_id
      WHERE json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.id') IN (${itemIds.map(() => '?').join(',')})
        AND v.voucher_date < ?
    `
    totalInitBalance += db.prepare(initSql).get(...itemIds, start_date).init_balance
  }
}
```

4. **鎵归噺鏁版嵁鏌ヨ**
```typescript
for (const [categoryCode, categoryItems] of itemsByCategory) {
  const batchSize = 900
  for (let i = 0; i < categoryItems.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = categoryItems.slice(i, i + batchSize)
    const itemIds = batch.map(item => item.id)

    const dataSql = `
      SELECT
        v.voucher_date,
        v.voucher_no,
        ve.account_code,
        ve.account_name,
        ve.summary,
        ve.direction,
        ve.amount,
        json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.id') as aux_id,
        json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.name') as aux_name,
        '${categoryCode}' as category_code,
        json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.field_values') as field_values_json
      FROM voucher_entries ve
      JOIN vouchers v ON v.id = ve.voucher_id
      WHERE json_extract(ve.aux_data, '$.${categoryCode}.id') IN (${itemIds.map(() => '?').join(',')})
        AND ... (鍏朵粬绛涢€夋潯浠?
      ORDER BY v.voucher_date, v.voucher_no, ve.seq
    `
    const entries = db.prepare(dataSql).all(...itemIds)
    allEntries.push(...entries)
  }
}
```

2. **閿欒鐨?UPDATE 璇彞**锛?   - 鍘熻Е鍙戝櫒灏濊瘯鏇存柊 UNINDEXED 鍒楋細`SET voucher_id = new.voucher_id`

**淇鏂规锛?*

浣跨敤 FTS5 鐨勭壒娈婂懡浠わ細`INSERT INTO fts_table(fts_table) VALUES('delete', rowid)`

```sql
-- 鍒犻櫎瑙﹀彂鍣紙浣跨敤鐗规畩鍛戒护锛?CREATE TRIGGER voucher_entries_fts_delete AFTER DELETE ON voucher_entries BEGIN
  INSERT INTO voucher_entries_fts(voucher_entries_fts, rowid, voucher_id, summary, account_code, account_name)
  VALUES('delete', old.rowid, old.voucher_id, COALESCE(old.summary, ''),
         old.account_code, old.account_name);
END;

-- 鏇存柊瑙﹀彂鍣紙鍏堝垹闄ゆ棫璁板綍锛屽啀鎻掑叆鏂拌褰曪級
CREATE TRIGGER voucher_entries_fts_update AFTER UPDATE ON voucher_entries BEGIN
  INSERT INTO voucher_entries_fts(voucher_entries_fts, rowid, voucher_id, summary, account_code, account_name)
  VALUES('delete', old.rowid, old.voucher_id, COALESCE(old.summary, ''),
         old.account_code, old.account_name);
  INSERT INTO voucher_entries_fts(rowid, voucher_id, summary, account_code, account_name)
  VALUES (new.rowid, new.voucher_id, COALESCE(new.summary, ''),
          new.account_code, new.account_name);
END;
```

**淇鐨勮Е鍙戝櫒锛?*
- `vouchers_fts_insert` - 鍑瘉鎻掑叆瑙﹀彂鍣?- `vouchers_fts_update` - 鍑瘉鏇存柊瑙﹀彂鍣?鉁?淇
- `vouchers_fts_delete` - 鍑瘉鍒犻櫎瑙﹀彂鍣?鉁?淇
- `voucher_entries_fts_insert` - 鍒嗗綍鎻掑叆瑙﹀彂鍣?- `voucher_entries_fts_update` - 鍒嗗綍鏇存柊瑙﹀彂鍣?鉁?淇
- `voucher_entries_fts_delete` - 鍒嗗綍鍒犻櫎瑙﹀彂鍣?鉁?淇

### 2. 鏂板鍑瘉鏃跺簭鎺у埗鍔熻兘

**淇敼鏂囦欢锛?*
- `client/src/views/system/Param.vue` - 绯荤粺鍙傛暟椤甸潰

**鍏蜂綋璇存槑锛?*

1. **鏈堝害缁撹浆鍒ゆ柇**锛?   - 姣旇緝涓婁竴寮犲嚟璇佺殑鏃ユ湡涓庡綋鍓嶆棩鏈?   - 濡傛灉鍦ㄥ悓涓€涓湀浠斤細瑙嗕负鏈仛鏈堝害缁撹浆

### 1. 鍒嗛〉鏍忕粍浠堕珮搴︿笉涓€鑷村交搴曚慨澶?

### 31. 淇鍑瘉鎵撳嵃锛氭棩鏈熴€侀噾棰濄€佸嚟璇佺被鍨嬪彇涓嶅埌鏁版嵁

**淇敼鏂囦欢锛?*
- `server/src/routes/voucher.ts`

**鍏蜂綋璇存槑锛?*

鎵撳嵃鎺ュ彛锛堝崟寮?`GET /voucher/print-data/:id` 鍜屾壒閲?`POST /voucher/print-data/batch`锛変娇鐢ㄤ簡閿欒鐨勬暟鎹簱瀛楁鍚嶏紝瀵艰嚧鏃ユ湡銆佸嚟璇佺被鍨嬨€佸€熻捶鍚堣鍏ㄩ儴涓虹┖銆?
淇鐨勫瓧娈垫槧灏勶細

| 閿欒鐢ㄦ硶 | 姝ｇ‘瀛楁 | 璇存槑 |
|---|---|---|
| `voucher.date` | `detail.voucher_date` | 鏁版嵁搴撳瓧娈靛悕涓?`voucher_date` |
| `voucher.voucher_type` | `detail.voucher_type_name` | 闇€ JOIN `voucher_types` 琛紝瀛楁鍚嶄负 `voucher_type_name` |
| `totals.debit/credit` | `totals.debitTotal/creditTotal` | `calculateVoucherTotals` 杩斿洖鐨勫瓧娈靛悕 |
| `entry.debit/credit` | `direction+amount` 杞崲 | 鍒嗗綍琛ㄥ瓨鐨勬槸 `direction('debit'/'credit') + amount`锛岄渶鎵嬪姩杞崲 |

鎵归噺鎺ュ彛鐨?SQL 涔熷悓姝ヤ慨澶嶏細`date` 鈫?`voucher_date`锛屽鍔?JOIN `voucher_types` 鑾峰彇鍑瘉绫诲瀷鍚嶇О銆?

   - 淇鏃фā鐗堜娇鐢ㄤ笉瀛樺湪鐨勫瓧娈电被鍨嬶紙voucher_seq 鈫?voucher_no锛寁oucher_date 鈫?date锛宎ttachment_count 鈫?attachments锛宼otal_amount 鈫?total_debit+total_credit锛宎mount_in_words 鈫?text锛宲reparer/reviewer/accountant 鈫?signature_maker/auditor/poster锛宻upervisor 鈫?signature_supervisor锛?   - 淇灞炴€у悕 textAlign 鈫?align锛團ieldElement 鎺ュ彛瀹氫箟浣跨敤 `align` 鑰岄潪 `textAlign`锛?   - 绉婚櫎涓嶅瓨鍦ㄧ殑 `visible` 灞炴€?   - 澧炲姞绾稿紶楂樺害浠?140mm 鍒?200mm锛堝師楂樺害涓嶈冻浠ュ绾虫墍鏈夊厓绱狅級

5. **鑴氭湰鍔熻兘锛?*
